Hu replied that he was unable to go due to illness. Since the Executive Yuan is in charge of government affairs, there is no need for everyone to go. Moreover, Sun is responsible for the cabinet, but he cannot implement the policies of resisting Japan and suppressing the Communists. Zhang is protected even though he lost troops and territory, and Sun has to resign. What can I do if I go to Nanking at this time? A representative said that Sun Yat-sen went north with illness in the 13th year of the Republic of China, why doesn't Mr. follow his example? Hu angrily said, "Today's government is not as good as Duan Qirui's. He did not dare to detain people, but now he actually detains them. Why do you send me into the tiger's mouth?" The representatives left without getting what they wanted. They will go north at 5:00 PM. The Jinda delegation of petitioners will leave the province and return north on the 28th. When they pass through Hong Kong, they will visit Hu again and stand vigil at Hu's residence until dawn to urge Hu to go. (Special dispatch on the 27th)

Military Department Issues a Circular Restricting the Organization of Volunteer Armies 29

(Nanking) The Ministry of Military Administration issued a circular to all Pacification Commissioners' Offices, Bandit Suppression Commissioners' Offices, and provincial and municipal governments, and a circular to all commanders-in-chief, division commanders, and commanders of garrisons, defense forces, fortresses, and military police, stating that in the future, the name of volunteer army, except for students of formal schools, local civil organizations shall not organize themselves without authorization, recruit soldiers and collect salaries, or appoint the names of military division and brigade commanders. If any of the above occurs, it should be stopped immediately. (Special dispatch on the 27th)

Page 9

Sino-German Joint Venture to Establish Steel Plant 32

The Ministry of Industry and Commerce Signs a Contract with a German Company

(Nanking) The Ministry of Industry and Commerce and the German Steel Company and affiliated companies signed a draft contract for a joint venture to establish the China National Steel Plant. The German representative was Mr.康道孚, and the Chinese representative was Minister of Industry and Commerce Chen Gongbo. The witnesses were Vice Ministers Guo Chuntao and Xu Xiqing, and the two directors of the Industry and Mining Department, Cheng Zhenjun and Yan Zhuang, and others. The contract contains 24 articles. The main points are: 1. To establish the China National Steel Plant and affiliated factories, and to mine coal and iron near the plant. 2. The capital is set at US$16 million to US$20 million, which is paid by Germany. 3. The output is stipulated to be 500 tons of pig iron per day, or its equivalent amount of steel, as the standard. 4. The management rights are completely controlled by the Chinese government, but the Chinese government may hire German experts as consultants. 5. After the draft contract is signed, the Chinese government may send students and engineers to Germany to work as interns in various factories and supervise the design and construction of various machines, and the expenses shall be borne by the German company. 6. All machinery, materials, and equipment, such as quality and price engineering, must be reviewed by China. 7. The plant construction project is scheduled to be completed in three years, and the German company is responsible for all projects. 8. The location is selected from Pukou or Wuhu, but must be decided after investigation by German engineers. 9. Repayment of the principal will begin in the fourth year from the start of construction, and it is stipulated that it will be repaid in installments over ten years, with a weekly interest rate of seven percent. 10. The plant is used as collateral. Before the plant is established, the Ministry of Finance will designate items as collateral. Within six months, both parties will sign and exchange a formal contract, and it is stipulated that construction of the plant building will begin within one year after the completion of the inspection. (Special dispatch on the 27th)

Ministry of Interior Plans to Implement Local Autonomy 33

(Nanking) In order to actively implement local autonomy, the Ministry of Interior ordered the Department of Civil Affairs to draft a plan, which will be implemented after approval. 1. The current County and City Organization Law is mostly unsuitable for the promotion of autonomy and should be revised by the Legislative Yuan. Then, the autonomy regulations at all levels should be revised according to the revised County and City Organization Law. 2. The Central Mass Movement Steering Committee and the Propaganda Committee are requested to compile propaganda publications on local autonomy. 3. Each province should establish an autonomy training institute, and each county and city should set up a branch to universally train autonomy talents. 4. The Ministry will send personnel to each province and city to supervise and inspect the results. 5. Each province should designate one or two counties as model counties for autonomy, and the county magistrate should be concurrently held by a member of the provincial government or a member of the provincial party headquarters. 6. Each province should complete county autonomy in stages according to the provincial and county situation in order to promote constitutional government. 7. Various cooperative laws and regulations should be formulated as soon as possible to develop the rural economy. (Special dispatch on the 27th)

(Hankou) On the 27th, bandits from Jiangxi were discovered in Huangling, Hanyang. A battalion of Qian Dajun's stationed troops fought unsuccessfully. Xu Tingyao's regiment and two battalions of Qian Dajun's troops have been dispatched to suppress them. (27th Special Dispatch)

Foreign News

Former British Foreign Secretary Henderson Gracefully Goes to Geneva 63

Not Giving Up Chairmanship of the Disarmament Conference

Reuters, London, 27th - Former Foreign Secretary Henderson departed today for Paris, then on to Geneva, to chair the Disarmament Conference, which will open next Monday. He was accompanied by his wife and secretary, Pike. Henderson's chairmanship of the Disarmament Conference is particularly noteworthy as he is neither a government official nor a member of Parliament. When he was Foreign Secretary in the Labour government, the League of Nations invited him to chair the Disarmament Conference. Although he later resigned from the post of Foreign Secretary, he has refused to relinquish the honor of chairing the Disarmament Conference. Despite efforts to persuade him to give it up, he has declined. The issue was raised in Parliament, and both MacDonald and Simon said it was not a matter for the British government to resolve but should be decided by the League of Nations, which had invited him to chair. Naturally, the League of Nations could not withdraw its invitation, and Henderson has thus gracefully departed. It is indeed unusual for someone holding this position to chair one of the world's most important conferences in recent years. Henderson recently suffered from an illness for four months but has now fully recovered.

Reuters, London, 27th - According to an official announcement, the list of the British delegation attending the Geneva Disarmament Conference on February 2nd is as follows: Prime Minister MacDonald, Foreign Secretary Simon, Colonial Secretary Thomas, Secretary of State for War Hailsham, Secretary of State for Air Londonderry, First Lord of the Admiralty Monsell, and Deputy Representative Lady Astor. The Prime Minister plans to attend the opening ceremony of Parliament on February 2nd before traveling to Geneva.

Meeting Between British and French Prime Ministers Postponed 64

National News, Paris, 27th - According to reliable sources in this morning's Petit Parisien, the meeting between the British and French Prime Ministers, which was scheduled for the end of next week, has been postponed because a common basis for their discussions could not be found. It is reported that negotiations between the British Finance Minister, Hore-Belisha, and representatives of the French Finance Ministry are continuing unabated, in the hope that a plan to reconcile their differences can be worked out before the Hoover Moratorium expires on June 30th of this year.

National News, Berlin, 26th - France is currently making every effort to extend the reparations conference until June 30th, which is just 24 hours away from the expiration of President Hoover's moratorium on debt payments. Since this news came from Paris, German newspapers have each had in-depth discussions on it. It is said that French Prime Minister Laval, Finance Minister Flandin, and British Ambassador to France Lord Tyrrell held a meeting in Paris yesterday, at which the French side made this proposal and, based on the French side's opinion, wanted to use this method to prepare for future negotiations between the French Prime Minister and British Prime Minister MacDonald. The tone of the French newspapers is that if the method advocated by France is adopted, the future reparations conference will have to immediately extend the current moratorium period. After Germany accepts the French proposal, it can only agree to the extension of the moratorium period. However, the extension of the moratorium period is tantamount to continuing to pay the unconditional annuities, a responsibility that Germany cannot continue to shoulder. Currently, the German government has stated that Germany should demand the early opening of the reparations conference so that all issues regarding reparations can be thoroughly considered before the expiration of the Hoover plan. If the French side insists on its own views, Germany can also express its views so that the truth can be revealed to the world.

Destroying Foreign Cloth and Gathering Crowds to Demonstrate

Havas, Bombay, 26th - Celebrations organized by the National Congress for Independence Day have caused disturbances. Crowds burned foreign textiles on a public road and threw stones at the police station. Police attacked the demonstrators with batons, and more than 50 people were injured. 72 people were arrested in the New Delhi area.

British Submarine Missing 66

Reuters, London, 27th - The submarine M2 has been missing since she submerged outside Portland at 10:30 yesterday morning. Her whereabouts have not been found so far, and it is feared that an accident has occurred. The submarine is carrying a small seaplane, 6 officers, and 48 crew members.

Havas, London, 27th - According to recent news, the location of the missing submarine M2 has been determined. Two destroyers dragged steel cables across the seabed and encountered an object that blocked the cable, which was determined to be the hull of the submarine. Several light boats have been ordered to proceed to the location with salvage equipment. Currently, the ships are anchored nearby, and a seaplane is flying over the sea for reconnaissance. However, all attempts to communicate with the missing submarine have been unsuccessful.

Since Japan re-imposed the ban on gold exports in November of the 12th year of the Republic, the amount of Japanese cash shipped to the United States, including this shipment, totals 89 million yen, to offset the former government's sales of US dollars in the United States. It is reported that the outstanding sales amount to 170 million yen. It is expected that this shipment of cash will be the last one.

Important News

Xi Qia Insists on Eliminating Bin County Provincial Government 70

Extreme Conditions Proposed at the Harbin Conference

Yushu County Has Been Captured by Ma Xilin

Harbin Correspondence: Jin Wuxuan, the representative sent by Xi Qia to Harbin to negotiate peace, left Harbin for Jilin at 8:00 AM yesterday. Xu Ziping, the representative of the Bin County Provincial Government, also returned to Bin on the same day. Negotiations between Jilin and Bin have thus completely broken down. Previously, Zhang Jinghui invited Cheng Yun to come to Harbin, but Cheng, being occupied, sent Xu Ziping, the Director of Finance, as his representative. Xi Qia's representative, Jin Wuxuan, expressed considerable dissatisfaction with this, believing that Xu had no full authority to resolve the matter. On the evening of the 17th, when the two sides met at the Administrative Chief's Office of the Special Zone, Jin Wuxuan proposed: (1) The Bin County Provincial Government must be abolished immediately and must not be moved elsewhere to be re-established. (2) All tax revenues from Jilin Province must be transferred to Jilin without interception en route. (3) No troops may be mobilized to take hostile actions against Jilin. (4) All military actions must be stopped immediately. (5) The safety of the families of all provincial officials must be guaranteed. Xu Ziping, considering the conditions to be too harsh and inconsistent with Zhang Jinghui's original intention of inviting them to negotiate, excused himself by saying that he needed to consult Cheng Yun and reply after receiving his instructions. The two sides stopped talks the next day. Upon hearing the report, Cheng Yun telegraphed Xu Ziping to cease negotiations and return to Bin County immediately. On the same day, Zhang Jinghui invited Jin Wuxuan alone and tried to persuade him to show some leniency and not be too demanding, but Jin refused, saying that he had received orders from Xi Qia when he came and that compromise was not possible without them. Therefore, Zhang was unable to mediate the situation and allowed the stalemate to continue. Although Jin spent several days in Harbin under the guise of meetings, he secretly contacted the two brigades of Ding Chao and Xing Zhanqing with great effort. Jin had previously served as Ding Chao's chief of staff and was particularly familiar with the middle and lower-ranking officers of Ding's troops, using both incentives and threats to considerable effect. Therefore, although the meeting was unsuccessful when he left Harbin, his activities in the army had already shown results. On the day Jin left Harbin, six generals, including Ding Chao, Li Du, Xing Zhanqing, Su Dechen, Zhang Zuozhou, and Feng Zhanhai, jointly telegraphed Xi Qia, saying that they were willing to submit to his control, but with two conditions: first, each would remain stationed in their original defenses without moving; and second, military expenses would be allocated monthly. Xi Qia has not yet replied to the telegram. These several generals are the pillars of the Bin County Provincial Government. If they are truly absorbed by Xi Qia, the Bin County Provincial Government will have no real strength and will be unable to survive. However, it is heard that Li Du and Feng Zhanhai have remained loyal to the Bin Provincial Government. Li's infantry battalion arrived in Bin County on the 20th to assist Feng's regiment in defending the provincial government. Bin County implemented martial law on the 20th, and the families of all important officials have moved to other counties. Cheng Yun has vowed to survive with the city or perish with the city. On the 19th, Cheng issued a telegram stating that regardless of how Xi Qia may press, he would never abolish the provincial government or move it elsewhere without a clear order from the central government and Zhang Auxiliary Marshal (Zuoxiang). If Xi Qia presses again, he will take appropriate self-defense measures. On the one hand, he also telegraphed Zhang Jinghui, saying that he found it difficult to accept the conditions proposed by Xi Qia's representative and had decided to lead the militia to defend the provincial government, even at the cost of sacrificing everything.

As for the military situation, since negotiations between the two sides broke down, the fighting became more intense. On the morning of the 18th, Ma Xilin's bandit army, along with more than 500 Japanese infantry and artillerymen who had arrived from Changchun, launched a fierce attack on Yushu County Regiment at 6:00 AM. The artillery fire was extremely intense, and the city walls were destroyed. The 25th Brigade of Zhang Zuozhou and the 26th Regiment of Song Wenjun did their best to defend the city, while the militia and police attacked Ma's left flank outside the city. However, due to the intense Japanese artillery fire, they were repulsed several times. At 9:00 AM on the 18th, three Japanese aircraft flew in from the Shulan County area, dropping bombs in the air. Various agencies in the city were destroyed, and order was disrupted. The bandits took the opportunity to loot, and merchants and residents cried and fled in despair. The 25th Brigade, unable to withstand the threat of the Japanese aircraft, was the first to collapse, withdrawing from the east gate and heading towards Wuchang. Song Wenjun's regiment was trapped in the city, with more than half of the soldiers killed or wounded. They only broke through at 10:00 AM and gathered at the Sanchahe station on the East Railway. Li Weicheng, the magistrate of Yushu County, escaped in disguise amidst the chaos, and his whereabouts are unknown. At 8:00 PM on the same day, Ma's troops safely led their forces into the city. After entering the city, the soldiers looted throughout the night until representatives from the Chamber of Commerce pleaded, and Ma Xilin finally ordered a halt. Since the evening of the 19th, Yushu has been under Xi Qia's control, and all news has been blocked. At 10:00 PM on the 19th, a branch of Ma's cavalry, numbering about 600, attacked Dehui. The area had no garrison troops, and the county magistrate ordered the militia and police to resist the bandits 15 li west of the city at Xiadianzi. They engaged in a fierce battle overnight, repelling the bandits at 2:00 AM on the morning of the 20th. However, Ma Xilin has now divided his troops into four directions: one branch harassing Sanchahe on the Dongtie-Hachang Line, another harassing Taolaizhao on the Hachang Line, and the majority moving towards Dehui. The county's forces are weak and without supplies, so it will be difficult to defend for long. After Yushu fell, Shuangcheng was only 140 li away, and Japanese aircraft flew over every day for reconnaissance. Panic reigned. On the 19th, Su Dechen, commander of the 22nd Defense Brigade, convened a meeting of local gentry, merchants, and police leaders. The majority advocated resistance. Su immediately sent Zhao's regiment under his command to deploy at Sanchahe, and also deployed his troops in conjunction with the militia around the city. On the 20th, a Japanese aircraft flew for reconnaissance and dropped many leaflets in the name of Yu Shenzheng, giving Su's brigade a deadline to surrender or retreat elsewhere, otherwise a general attack would be launched. Yesterday, it was heard that Yu's cavalry had reached the Hongqitou village south of Shuangcheng, and they will inevitably come into contact with Su's brigade today or tomorrow. Yu Shenzheng's main force, numbering about 10,000, plus several hundred Japanese cavalry and artillery, launched a general attack on Wuchang County on the evening of the 19th. The First Regiment of Xing Zhanqing's brigade stationed there, along with two battalions of Feng Zhanhai's troops and the militia, resisted the enemy together. The fighting was fierce. The Japanese army used three armored vehicles to cover Yu's army and launched several fierce attacks on the east city at 11:00 PM on the 19th, leveling the trenches. Fortunately, Feng's troops resisted with all their might and have not yet been lost. This morning, Ding Chao ordered two infantry battalions under his command to rush to reinforce, and they are expected to arrive tomorrow. Yu's army is now attacking that direction with all its forces, believing that if Wuchang falls, Acheng will be difficult to defend, and the Bin County Provincial Government will lose its shield and cannot exist. Recently, the Acting Chairman of Bin Province, Cheng Yun, has issued a proclamation to the militias of various counties to quickly form volunteer armies to protect the provincial government. Shuangcheng, Acheng, Fuyu, Zhuhe and other counties have replied that they have formed the armies and will listen to orders. (20th)

Zhang Jinghui Replaces Special Zone Officials 71

Harbin City KMT Headquarters Also Sealed

Harbin Correspondence: At the request of the Japanese side, Zhang Jinghui dismissed Wang Ruihua, the Director of the Special Police Management Office, on the 14th of this month and replaced him with Jin Ronggui. Jin served as the Director of the Special Police Office in the 11th and 16th years of the Republic and still has credibility with the Russian overseas community. Therefore, after he took office, the Russian overseas community ended its violent actions. However, the Japanese side requested the removal of Zang Qifang, Director of the Land Bureau, Zhou Shouyi, Director of the Education Department, and Xu Zhen, Director of the Telephone Bureau, along with Wang Ruihua. Although Zhou and Zang submitted their resignations recently, they were ordered to stay yesterday. Xu, however, was approved for dismissal. At the same time, the city KMT headquarters was ordered to close down, and its former site was occupied by the Harbin Office of the Heilongjiang Army. From now on, all institutions in Harbin will be completely monolithic. Xu Zhen's position, though nominally the Director of the Telephone Bureau, actually controls all wired and wireless long-distance telephones. Today, he held a handover with the new Director, Fan Pei. I visited Mr. Xu, who said that he had come to Harbin to take office as Director of the Telephone Bureau under the orders of the Northeast Transportation Committee, originally hoping to thoroughly reorganize the Harbin telecommunications administration. Unexpectedly, since taking office, he has been running around and has not been able to start the reorganization, as he immediately encountered a period of turmoil. It has been more than four months since the September 18th Incident. In these four months, he has continued to work hard in the original spirit, relying on communication to transmit domestic and foreign news, and therefore incurred resentment. Now, Jin Biedong, the Director of the New Northeast Telecommunications Administration, plans to unify telecommunications administration in the Northeast and has sent two consultants and counselors to Harbin to handle the issue of the Harbin telecommunications administration's affiliation. The reason why he has submitted his resignation is that Director Zhang appreciates him very much and has retained him in this position, but he must be under the command of the New Northeast Telecommunications Administration. If he agrees, there is no problem. However, as he is under the Ministry of the government, he is unable to obey, so he has decided to resign. As for the rumors in the city that Director Zhang dismissed him for administrative convenience, they are purely fictitious. In the future, he will only retire and not ask about current affairs. (January 20th)

Tianjin Tram Fare Increase Uproar 72

Citizens Rise Up to Express Opposition

All Tramcars Stop Running for the Entire Day

Pretext Used to Reinforce Troops in the City

Tianjin Correspondence: The Tianjin Tram and Electric Light Enterprise was established in the twenty-third year of the Guangxu reign of the Qing Dynasty, through a contract signed by the Minister of Beiyang, Yuan Shikai, with the Belgian Consul in Tianjin, Mr. Ga De'er, the Shanghai Yanghang manager, Hai Zha, and the engineer, Sha Te. It was contracted to be managed by Belgian merchants. In November of the sixteenth year of the Republic of China, our authorities, citing numerous breaches of contract by the Belgian company, such as extending routes beyond the stipulated limits and engaging in motor power operations, as well as arbitrarily deducting large sums from surplus profits to expand assets and thereby reduce the reported tax amount, lodged a serious protest through the Tianjin Electricity Supervision Office. At that time, it was even planned to take over the tram and electric light company. Subsequently, the consuls-general of Japan, France, and Italy in Tianjin stepped in to mediate, negotiating a peaceful resolution to correct the company's breaches of contract and increase the annual tax revenue to our country. The matter was then settled. Currently, the company's annual surplus profit is approximately four to five million yuan. Last year, Tianjin experienced two incidents, during which the company suspended tram service for over ten days, resulting in losses of tens of thousands of yuan. The company suddenly proposed compensating for these losses, and on January 1st of this year, without the consent of the municipal government, unilaterally increased the fare by two copper coins per ticket. Tianjin merchants and residents, citing the post-turmoil period and the economic hardship of the people, particularly the lower and middle classes who rely on tram travel, expressed strong opposition. The first to propose this opposition were the district chiefs of all eight autonomous districts in the city. Subsequently, workers from various labor unions also recognized that the tram fare increase would significantly impact workers' transportation costs. They organized "Committees Against the Tram Fare Increase" and formed a 150-member picket team. Each day, they went to various tram lines to deliver speeches, urging passengers not to buy tickets until the tram fare increase issue was resolved. Simultaneously, they requested the municipal government to severely reprimand the company and stop the fare increase to protect the people's livelihood. Acting Mayor Zhou Longguang immediately, based on public opinion, instructed the company to cancel the fare increase and await review. However, the company's attitude was extremely rigid, ignoring the instruction. They claimed that the fare increase was based on the contract and did not violate it, requesting the Chinese side to abide by the agreement (as the contract stipulated the possibility of increasing the fare to five cents). The municipal government, however, maintained that this public utility concerned the livelihood of all citizens and that, regardless of the contract's stipulations, prior consent from the local government should have been obtained. The fare increase was implemented without municipal government approval, constituting a serious procedural error and therefore being illegal. There was no room for negotiation unless the fare increase was first canceled. Subsequently, the company requested the Belgian Consul in Tianjin to repeatedly negotiate with Wang Shuchang, Chairman of the Hebei Provincial Government, and Zhang Xueliang, Director of the Peiping Pacification Office, to approve the fare increase. For over twenty days, the matter remained unresolved due to strong public sentiment. Consequently, the picket team's dispatch led the tram company to order the trams to stop running. Once the picket team withdrew, the trams would resume service. Thus, in recent days, tram service in the Chinese district has been intermittent, causing great hardship to the citizens. The other day, a conflict arose between the picket team of the Committee Against the Fare Increase and the tram ticket seller, Liu Ruirong. The picket team severely beat Liu Ruirong and slightly injured dozens of others. The tram workers, totaling over six hundred, seeing that they could not perform their duties and that operating in the Chinese district posed a constant danger, decided to unanimously strike yesterday morning, completely halting all tram services in the city. Simultaneously, they presented five demands to the labor union, including punishing the picket team and ensuring the safety of tram workers. However, the citizens, unaware of the true situation and amidst this period of unsettled nerves, became increasingly suspicious. As for the situation in the city, due to transportation disruptions, pedestrian traffic was extremely congested. The Japanese Consul also expressed concerns about the security of the Japanese concession, repeatedly inquiring about the situation to the municipal government, stating that the tram stoppage greatly affected the Japanese district and that, if necessary, troops would be deployed at the northern end of Asahi Street to maintain order. The municipal government, realizing the gravity of the situation, dispatched Secretary Lü Jin to negotiate with the tram labor union, requesting the immediate restoration of transportation. The labor union then presented seven demands for the municipal government to fulfill. If the municipal government agreed to implement them, work would resume immediately: (1) Requesting the municipal government to promptly resolve the tram fare increase issue; (2) Immediately apprehending Liu Butong, the instigator who incited the picket team to beat the workers; (3) Dissolving the picket team, which, under the guise of opposing the tram fare increase, was actually disrupting local security, and arresting its leaders, Ding Yutian, Li Jingshan, He Xiqian, Zhang Zhongqi, and Shen Hongrun; (4) Confiscating the murderous weapons stored within the municipal party headquarters; (5) Strictly ordering the Public Security Bureau to dispatch a team to be permanently stationed at the picket team's office to monitor the picket team's regrouping; (6) Ordering Liu Butong to compensate the injured workers for medical expenses and all losses; (7) Reserving the right to prosecute Liu Butong for his criminal liability. Representative Lü expressed acceptance. At 5:30 PM, labor union directors Chen Zelin and Zhang Guangxing reported the results of the negotiations with the municipal government to the workers. The workers, considering the urgency of the external diplomatic situation, agreed to resume work first. By about 6:00 PM, all trams in the city were running, and transportation gradually returned to normal. Today, the trams are operating as usual. The labor union has dispatched representatives to the municipal government, requesting the implementation of the proposed seven conditions. Mayor Zhou Longguang personally met with them, stating that within the realm of possibility, he would implement them immediately and ordered the Public Security Bureau to arrest the picket team should they regroup. It seems that this fare increase storm can be resolved within days. (January 25th)

Suzhou 74

Lake Bandits Rob Two Villages in One Night Xielu , the fifth district of Hengjing, a county subordinate, was suddenly attacked by thirty to forty lake bandits at about 9 PM the other day. They spoke with a Hakka accent and carried firearms and other weapons. After arriving in the village, they swarmed into the home of the widow, Xi Lu, looting it and abducting Lu's eldest son, Nian, and second son, Genfu, leaving behind a letter demanding a ransom of one thousand yuan. After the robbery, they fled towards Taihu Lake. At about 12 PM, another large group of lake bandits arrived, looting house by house, abducting Deputy Village Chief Lin Zeqing and villagers Zhou Qianchu, Zhou Qianchu's two young sons Zhou Baixiang, his wife Weng, Zhou Jingqing's eldest daughter-in-law Shen, third daughter-in-law Xu, Gui Xu's daughter, and two children. They also shot and injured villager Wu Zhou. They later fled towards Taihu Lake. After the incident, the police team stationed there pursued them without success and reported to the brigade headquarters for handling.

A Large Number of Japanese Residents Leave Suzhou for Shanghai The Japanese Consul stationed in Suzhou, Kawanami Shoichi, visited County Chief Wu at the County Government yesterday (27th) morning with interpreter Lin Jia, saying that due to the serious situation in Shanghai, he requested protection for the lives and property of Japanese residents in Suzhou. County Chief Wu replied that he would do his best to protect the lives and property of Japanese residents in Suzhou and hoped to inform the Japanese residents not to misunderstand. Kawanami expressed satisfaction and then took his leave. It is also understood that in addition to the special police station established earlier by the Public Security Bureau near the Japanese Concession, the 60th Division has specially dispatched a platoon of soldiers to be stationed in the Hongmiao Temple for protection. Furthermore, it is understood that on the 26th, the Japanese Consulate received a telegram from the Japanese Consulate in Shanghai ordering all Japanese residents in Suzhou to leave Suzhou and concentrate in Shanghai. Yesterday (27th) morning at 8:43 AM, the Changhu train No. 20 departing from Suzhou already had a group of over eighty Japanese residents leaving Suzhou for Shanghai.

Wuxi 75

Hwa Yih Sock Factory Suddenly Burns Down The Huigong Bridge approach on Tonghui Road outside the North Gate, behind the silk factory, the Hwa Yih Sock Factory, suddenly caught fire at 2:30 AM yesterday, and the flames quickly spread through the roof and became uncontrollable. Subsequently, upon receiving the alarm, the local fire brigade rushed to the scene to put out the fire, rescuing seventy-one sock knitting machines. In the end, twenty-three houses were burned down. During the height of the fire, an old woman living upstairs, with no way to escape, jumped from the building, resulting in serious injuries from the fall. The cause of the fire is quite strange.

A Murder Case in Kaihua Township Resolved Xue Jukang, a Daoist from Jinxi Bridge in Tu 73 of Kaihua Township in the 14th District, went to the home of Dong Pan across the river on the 23rd of this month to attend a funeral, when he suddenly got into a brawl with Dong A'da, Dong A'zhu, and Rende (mistakenly reported as Qin in yesterday’s news), resulting in serious injuries and death. After receiving the news, the County Court Prosecutor's Office sent Prosecutor Du to the village on the afternoon of the 25th for an autopsy. Because it was already late, the autopsy was postponed. So on the morning of the 26th, they led Wang, the forensic official, and bailiffs to the village for the autopsy. The autopsy revealed that the deceased Xue Jukang had three fractured ribs on the left side of his body and a contusion on the right side of his body. There was a contusion on the scrotum and the scrotum was swollen several times. The autopsy concluded that Xue Jukang had been beaten to death. After the autopsy, it was ordered that the family of the deceased prepare a coffin for burial and that the village chief Hu Ronggen turn over the suspects Dong Pan et al. within three days to be dealt with according to the law.

Changshu 76

Bandits Impersonate Soldiers and Detain Ship There is a ferry service operating between Dongtang Town and Kunshan in this county. In the afternoon the other day, the Jiatan E ship of the Yongli Shipping Bureau was approaching Dongtang Town when over one hundred armed soldiers suddenly arrived at the town carrying guns and claiming that they were under orders to suppress bandits and had come to detain the ship. The townspeople were not suspicious at the time. It was not until 3 PM, when the Jia'e ship arrived at the port, that the armed men went aboard the ship, drove the passengers ashore, then boarded the ship themselves and ordered the captain to sail into the lake. The incident was learned by the 14th Water Police Team stationed near Dangkou. The water police team went to investigate and learned that they were not regular soldiers. When asked, the local people did not see any unit number either. They immediately telegraphed Shen, the district chief of the 3rd Water Police District of Suzhou. Upon hearing the news, Shen immediately dispatched a team to Yangcheng Lake to launch an attack from both sides with the 14th Team in order to eliminate the bandits.

Zhenjiang 77

A Robbery Occurs Near Changshan Huang Yiquan, who owns a tofu shop near Changshan ten miles from Zhenjiang, is no longer young. Because he is usually thrifty, he can be said to be well-fed. Unexpectedly, he was coveted by bandits. At the third watch the other night, when the Huang family was all asleep, more than ten bandits broke into the house and robbed him of nine silver dollars and seventy-three thousand copper coins. They also smashed two tofu vats. Huang was heartbroken by this robbery. He has reported the incident to the local village security and requested a search.

Beating Grandmother and Being Detained and Punished Huang Erhun, who lives at No. 6 Sanshan Lane in this city, is by nature rude, savage, and abnormal. Yesterday afternoon, he had a verbal argument with his uncle over something. The grandmother intervened to mediate. Huang, considering his grandmother to be meddling, grabbed the teapot from the table and hit his grandmother's head violently, causing her to bleed profusely and collapse to the ground. The neighbors were all indignant and reported the incident to the local police, who took Huang to the bureau for punishment.

Yangzhou 78

Verdict Announced in the Case of a Police Officer Abusing His Position The case of Chen Lu, Director of the First Branch of the Jiangdu Public Security Bureau, for abusing his position has concluded. Prosecutor Ju Dongcai of the court filed a public lawsuit charging him with fourteen counts of abusing his position and fraud. After repeated trials, which lasted for more than eight months, the verdict was finally announced in the first instance yesterday (25th). Chen Lu, Dong Zhaolu, and Xia Ruiqing were all found not guilty. Zhao Huanzhen, Jiang Futian, and Han Wenlong were each fined forty yuan for gambling. Furthermore, the case of Lu Haifan and others, special agents of the Public Security Bureau, forging official documents and extorting opium from the Xu family has been concluded after investigation and trial by the court. Today (26th), the convicts were again brought before the court, and the judge announced the sentence. Lu Haishen was sentenced to six months of imprisonment, Wang Xi was sentenced to one year of imprisonment, Shen Bangrui, Xu Rong, and Wei Zhuo were each sentenced to six months of imprisonment, with a three-year suspended sentence, Li Jun was sentenced to one year and two months of imprisonment, and Tang Bichen was sentenced to one month of imprisonment and a fine of ten yuan. However, Lu, Wang, Li, Tang, and other four people disagreed with the verdict and planned to appeal.

Important Educational News

Suzhou Middle School Association Petitions the Executive Yuan for Education Funding 79

Teachers' Association Resigns En Masse to the China Middle School Association

The Suzhou Middle School Association and the Teachers' Association sent a telegram to the Nanjing Executive Yuan addressed to President Sun and all members of the Council stating: "The dispute over Suzhou education funding and the Central University funding can only be resolved if the Ministry of Finance bears the full cost of Central University. If temporary measures are taken and compromises are made, it will inevitably lead to disturbances and eventually ruin everyone. We pledge not to recognize this. The Suzhou Middle School Association and Teachers' Association kowtow."

The Suzhou Middle School Association replied to the China Middle School Association's letter of resignation stating: "We have received your letter dated January 14th stating that in order to support the Provincial Government's proposal to cease the allocation of Central University funding, you intend to submit a collective resignation to our Association. We have investigated that the provisional budget regulations issued by the Central Government in the nineteenth year stipulated that national taxes should fund national schools and provincial taxes should fund provincial schools. The boundary is extremely clear. Central University occupies provincial taxes because of historical reasons. Now, it has become a habit that cannot be changed. The resolution of the third meeting of the Executive Yuan clearly contradicts the aforementioned regulations. If Suzhou Province is forever burdened with this, it will undoubtedly lead Suzhou education to its death. Your opinion is extremely admirable. In addition to having our entire Association petition the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Education, and the Provincial Government for consideration, we have also issued a declaration seeking public opinion and appealing to the Executive Yuan to argue our case reasonably. We will always follow the same path as your Association in the hope of extending the fate of our province's education. In the event that things do not go as desired and the goal is not achieved, we will also be unable to take responsibility and will have the same attitude as all of you, stepping aside for more capable individuals. However, at this time of uncertainty, we still rely on joint efforts to proceed and cannot be passive. Therefore, your opinion on collective resignation should be temporarily withdrawn. We are in the same boat through thick and thin, and our friendship is crucial to mutual support. We look forward to your cooperation. This is addressed to the Jiangsu Provincial Middle School Teachers' Association. Sincerely, the Jiangsu Provincial Middle School Association, January 24th."

The Military Teachers' Association sent a letter of resignation to the China Middle School Association stating: "We are writing to inform you that at the Provincial Government meeting on January 8th, a resolution was passed to cease the allocation of Central University funding by the Jiangsu Education Funding Management Office, which is a fundamental solution to the Suzhou education funding problem. Upon reading the resolution of the third meeting of the Executive Yuan of the National Government, that the Suzhou Education Funding Management Office should permanently allocate 1.32 million yuan in annual funding to Central University, it is tantamount to leading Suzhou education to its death. It is clear that national taxes should fund national schools and provincial taxes should fund provincial schools. The reasons are very sufficient. The remedial measures for Suzhou education funding proposed by Director Zhou are very important. At the emergency meeting of the Provisional Representative Assembly of our Association on the afternoon of January 13th, it was decided that whether or not Suzhou Province ceases the allocation of Central University funding is related to the fate of secondary education in the entire province. Therefore, in addition to issuing a declaration to the outside world and publicly recommending representatives to petition in Beijing, in order to support the resolution of the Provincial Government, our Association will submit a collective resignation to your Association. This letter is to inform you and we hope you will take it into consideration. This is addressed to the Jiangsu Provincial Middle School Association. Sincerely, the Jiangsu Provincial Middle School Teachers' Association, January 14th."

The Department of Education immediately forwarded the request to the Provincial Government and attached its opinion that in view of the province's depleted treasury, the establishment of an education garden was actually beyond its means, but in order to commemorate the martyrs and protect the cemetery, it seemed appropriate to start by planting trees in the garden and proposed to change the name of the garden to the Jiangxi Martyrs Cemetery Forest Garden.

The Prelude to the East Asian Art Exposition 86

Gao Jianfu is Highly Welcomed Internationally

The Art Community Holds Meetings to Research

Gao Jianfu, a famous calligrapher from Guangdong, returned to Calcutta from the Himalayas and then went to the Lion Country (Colombo) to promote Chinese culture and study the Theravada Buddhism there. He reportedly gave a lecture on Buddhist art at the Buddhist Association of Ceylon yesterday, which was attended by many people. He later opened an art exhibition at the Young Men's Buddhist Association in Bolina for five days. People from various countries came to visit in droves. This is the first time that Chinese art has entered the territory of Ceylon, so there was such enthusiasm. The art community was stimulated by this kind of approach, and the atmosphere suddenly changed. Various associations were set up to study the art, and it was agreed that this kind of Chinese art is truly the light of our Eastern culture and needs to be developed together. After the meeting, those who heard the news and arrived late were disappointed. They earnestly requested the association to ask Gao to hold another exhibition to satisfy the audience and planned to continue it for three more days starting tomorrow. It is also reported that Gao has jointly prepared a pan-Asian art exposition with various art groups in Ceylon and India and plans to hold it in India in the fall of next year.

Sports

Shen Siliang Discusses Participation in the Davis Cup 92

Gold Price Too High, Funding Difficulties

Cannot Wait Until Next Year

Hopes for Establishment of New Asian Zone

Australia Changes to American Zone

Regarding the Davis Cup World Tennis Tournament, there was talk last year of establishing an Asian Zone, including countries such as China, the Philippines, Australia, India, Japan, and Malaysia. Australian Davis Cup veteran Brookes strongly advocated for this. When he went to Manila, he met with Philippine Governor Davis, the initiator of the cup, and presented the cup. Brookes argued that currently there are only European and American zones, and it is too costly in terms of time and money for Asian and Eastern countries to travel long distances to Europe and America to participate. Moreover, there are many Asian countries, so the reasoning is very sound. The Philippine Governor seemed to agree, but this year it has not been realized. According to Australian news, Australia was originally scheduled to join the Asian Zone this year, but since it has not been established, it has changed to the American Zone. During the last board meeting of the National Sports Association, there was a proposal by Lin Qiu to participate in this year's Davis Cup, so a special inquiry was made to Secretary-General Shen Siliang for his opinion. Shen said that with the current high price of gold, it is difficult for China to participate in the Davis Cup unless private individuals and the government can provide donations and assistance. If the Asian Zone is established, he will do his best to ensure China participates every year, as it will be more economical and easier to plan. Therefore, he strongly hopes it can be realized. Now that the new zone is not established for the time being, China's participation can only be postponed until next year.

Results of Last Night's Basketball Games: Qingguang and Xiqing Both Win 93

Qingguang Defeats Zhenru...45 to 33

The Shanghai Basketball Association had a total of four matches last night. The game between Qingguang and Zhenru was the most intense. The details of each game are as follows:

Qingguang Turns Defeat into Victory 94

Qingguang was briefly dimmed. Huang Zhaolin scored one free throw and one regular basket for Zhenru, putting them ahead 4-0. Qingguang's Tan Daling then scored a free throw, followed by a basket after Cai Rongrui of the opposing team mistakenly passed the signal. As the score narrowed, the lead changed hands frequently. Zhenru's center Chen Jinzhi showed quick footwork, accurately shooting four baskets, relying on his strength to maintain Zhenru's momentum. At that time, Qingguang's steps were chaotic and their defense was scattered, resulting in a score of 16-19 at halftime.

Zhenru lost momentum after the opening, with Yu Xuanzi scoring one basket. Qingguang seized the opportunity, with Tan adding two points, turning defeat into victory. Yang Shuhui and Yin Guiren each scored three points. Qingguang's Zhang Jinlin made a long-range shot, tying the score at 22. After this change, the situation for Qingguang and Zhenru changed dramatically, one side recovering its old form, the other declining after its peak. Within five minutes, Qingguang scored ten consecutive points, and Zhenru became a spent force, unable to do anything. In the end, Qingguang won 45-33, with Shao Ji as the referee.

Donghua Won Against Lehua Yesterday 98

2-0 Group A Match

Two Goals in the First Half, Draw in the Second Half

The Lehua football team lost 0-2 to Donghua at the baseball field yesterday afternoon. Many people still came to watch. The formations of the two teams were as follows:

Chen Hongguang Opens the Scoring First 99

Referee He Chunhui blew the silver whistle, and Donghua kicked off, immediately adopting an aggressive offensive, reaching the goal. After hovering several times, Dai Linjing turned and saved a shot beautifully and accurately, flying towards the goal. Just when everyone thought it would go in, Lu Jin'en calmly caught it. They fought evenly matched for more than ten minutes. Li Yichen dribbled the ball up to the defensive line, dodged, and passed to Qian Jingyong. Arriving again at the goal, Lu Zhongen signaled Weng Kefa to kick it out, but an airborne general came from the sky. Chen Hongguang had already run up and shot it in.

Tu Kaiyuan Scores Another One 100

Li wanted to attack but couldn't. Tu Kaiyuan watched coldly from the sidelines, seeing the opportunity, and kicked it in. The first half ended with a score of 2-0.

In the second half, Lehua's situation remained dull, with no hope of opening up. Heavily stacked, it was full of Donghua's army within five steps, full of enemy traces. Dai Linjing Shows Mercy 102

Originally, they were family, why be so ruthless? Donghua originally came from Lehua, so show some affection. This is why Dai Linjing's penalty kick did not score. Finally, Sun Huipei charged at Chen Pu in the penalty area, and referee He did not show any mercy, awarding a penalty kick, which was kicked by Dai Linjing, lightly swept, and went to the side, ending it like this.

Free Talk

National Crisis Conference and Celebrity Conference (Part 1) 106

The purpose of the National Crisis Conference is to resolve the national crisis. This can be inferred from the name itself. However, the powers have not been announced, the methods have not been clarified, and the people involved cannot understand it clearly, let alone the general public, which is even more vague. But one thing has been published in black and white: the list of appointed members announced by the Executive Yuan.

Let's try to study this list. Regardless of how different these members' past histories are, or how opposed their current political views are, they all have one thing in common: they are all celebrities - famous people, whose names have been displayed in newspapers and cherished in the pockets of the authorities. The main component of this National Crisis Conference is celebrities. The National Crisis Conference can only be considered a celebrity conference, at most a conference of celebrities presenting suggestions for resolving the national crisis. It can't even be called an expert conference, because many of them are not experts.

The fundamental mistake of this list lies not in what it includes, but in what it omits - in the complete absence of those who should be there. No one can deny that the vast majority of the owners of the Republic of China are farmers and workers. Can we find a farmer who actually tills the land himself or a worker who actually does manual labor himself in this list? When the national crisis is at hand, how can we break through this difficult situation if we don't invite the vast majority of the owners to personally resolve it?

Some people say that the appointed members can all lay down their butcher knives and become Buddhas on the spot, meaning everyone can speak for the common people. The politics of recent years have been ruined by this word "substitute." First, they speak for the common people, then they eat for the common people, and finally they govern for the common people, leaving the common people first with nowhere to speak, then with no way to eat, and finally with no power to protect the country. Substitute! I wish the dictionary of the Republic of China would not have this heartbreaking word tomorrow!

Military Pigeons Did Not Originate in Japan 107

— Leishi

The Daily News reported a dispatch from Tianjin. The Japanese army recently transported more than two hundred carrier pigeons from the country to test their communication effectiveness in Shenyang, Shanhaiguan, and Tianjin. Flying from Shenyang to Tianjin takes two and a half hours, and from Shanhaiguan to Tianjin takes one hour. Some say that the Japanese are clever and quick-witted, and in addition to police dogs, they also have military pigeons. Little do they know that military pigeons were not invented by the Japanese. We used to have them often in our country. They were initially used to transmit information, and then extended to military use. Now, I will briefly list one or two examples from ancient books to dispel the erroneous view of being shocked by everything foreign while destroying our own spirit.

"Anecdotes of the Tianbao Era" states that Zhang Jiuling raised many pigeons at home when he was young. Whenever he had correspondence with relatives and friends, he would tie the letters to the pigeons' feet and they would fly to the instructed place. They were called "flying slaves." According to this, they already existed in the Tang Dynasty, but they were not used for military purposes.

"History of the Song Dynasty: Biography of Xia State" states that during the Qingli period of Emperor Renzong, Sang Yi was征服(conquering) Yuan Wu. On the way, he obtained several silver mud boxes with sounds of movement inside. He did not dare to open them. The chief commander Ren Fu arrived and opened them. There were more than a hundred pigeons with whistles hanging from them. They rose from the middle and circled above the army. Thereupon, the Xia soldiers converged from all directions. Fu fought bravely and the army was destroyed. According to this, they were used for military purposes.

"Qidong Yeyu" states that Zhang Jun inspected Qu Duan's army and found no one there. Zhang was surprised and said he wanted to review them. Duan presented the registers of the five armies under his command. Zhang ordered him to review one of the armies, so he opened a cage in the courtyard and released a pigeon. The army being reviewed arrived immediately. Zhang was astonished. Later, he wanted to see all of them, so he released all five pigeons, and the five armies gathered in an instant, with shining armor and bright flags. According to this, it also happened during the Song Dynasty. Perhaps military pigeons originated in the Song Dynasty?

Moreover, they also existed in modern times. During the Hong Yang Rebellion, when Zeng Guoquan besieged Nanjing, his brother Guofan, as the imperial envoy stationed in Anqing, used pigeons to transmit daily reports in the army. This is mentioned in Zhu Mei'an's book "Trivia from a Guest Window." It is said that he raised hundreds of pigeons.

Blind Woman 109

— Yi Zang

There is an old woman in Lotus Pond, Hangzhou. She is blind and her husband died early. She struggles to make ends meet. However, she is very intelligent and has learned to calculate the five elements. She is determined and diligent. Before a year is over, she has thoroughly mastered the two trillion four hundred and forty-five billion five elements and six lines. When she talks to people about fortune and misfortune, she is always accurate. Therefore, her door is like a market. Officials and scholars come to resolve their doubts in an endless stream. Commoners and foolish women from the streets wait outside her door every day at dawn to ask for fortunes, often numbering in the hundreds. The divination fee is two jiao, and the registration fee is twelve copper coins, in the order of the lottery tickets obtained upon entering the door. Therefore, they often fight to grab lottery tickets when the door is opened. After obtaining a lottery ticket, they are allowed to enter the divination altar. On the altar is the divination deity, and below are four long benches that can accommodate twenty to thirty people. The number of people served in the morning is limited to thirty. It is not possible to get a number in place of someone else. In the afternoon, those from afar are served, with fees ranging from five to ten yuan. She can earn a hundred gold a day and now has assets of one hundred thousand. A certain director-general heard of this and was surprised. One day, he secretly sent a clerk to greet her, asking about future fortunes and misfortunes. The old woman finished calculating the five elements and frowned, stomping her feet and saying, "This person's fate has too many earth branches and heavenly stems. There is no doubt of corruption. Although there is much wealth, it is weak. The wife has great power. This year, the earth element is more obscure, transforming the hurting officer into Máo. Although collecting wealth is satisfying, the heavenly luck is ending. He will definitely suffer a great disaster. If he does not stop his corruption, retire early, cultivate his mind, and do good, disaster will be imminent." The director-general was shocked and lost color upon hearing this, angered by her irresponsible remarks and driving her out. The old woman left in disappointment. The director-general was also uneasy. He considered that the effect was uncertain. However, for the sake of fame and profit, he remained reluctant to leave his position. Before long, his son suddenly suffered a kidnapping and had to be ransomed for five hundred thousand yuan. In less than a few months, he was also dismissed from his position and imprisoned. Only then did he believe the old woman's words, which were completely accurate. Previously, when the director-general was the director-general of a certain province, he exploited in every possible way and was unusually corrupt. His wife, a certain Ms. Soong, was by nature悍泼. Many of the officials in the government office were her relatives. Those who wanted to seek a position had to bribe the wife with a thousand gold and agree to a four-six split of the profits. There was a certain Mr. Zhang from Hubei who sought a tax position but had no connections. He spared no expense and asked people to lobby for him. Unexpectedly, the matter was leaked and detected by a certain official. The director-general was implicated and imprisoned, and his property was confiscated. He soon died of illness.

Going to War 110

— A Member of the Youth Aid Horse Corps, First Regiment

(14) Brief Summary of Beijing-Ping

We set off from Jinling University in the capital on the morning of December 28th last year and arrived in Beiping on the afternoon of January 3rd this year. It took six days and nights, passing through four provinces, a total of more than 2,300 li. Along the way, we braved the wind and snow, waking up early and sleeping early, living a simple life. Although we took vehicles along the way, who would willingly endure this hardship if it were not for saving the country? Fortunately, our ambition to kill the enemy will soon be rewarded, and our full of blood will not stop boiling.

Just as we were about to set off from Beijing to the north, we encountered a heavy snow. At the same time, the temperature dropped sharply, and it was extremely cold. Although we don't know how many degrees below zero on the thermometer, most of the comrades have been unable to bear it. After discussions by the cadres, everyone believed that the wind and snow ahead would be even more severe and the journey would be even more difficult. It was decided to temporarily station the entire team in Pukou.

Images of a Trip to the North and Other Things (9) 111

— Yao Sufeng

A Self-Account by Movie Star Hu Die

On a winter evening when slanting winds and drizzle suddenly intertwined, the Beijing-Shanghai train sent us back to Shanghai. Shanghai was still bustling and bustling, no different from before we went to Beiping. But we brought back some real terror from the north, and we still felt somewhat alienated.

At the same time, our alienation is just like the alienation of others. China is originally a group that is mutually alienated, mutually suspicious, mutually distrustful, mutually destructive, mutually deceptive, and mutually engaged in things that harm others and do not benefit oneself. We are also considered unfortunate to live in such an environment, so even someone as small as I am cannot escape all kinds of rumors and slander beyond imagination.

I always think this way: Why does society treat women so harshly? I have suffered all kinds of treatment, and there are often many things that I don't know about, but others seem to spread them as if they were absolutely true. Under this kind of treatment and encounter, it is really not easy to live. If I ignore it, it will add to the ridicule. If I try to defend myself, it seems that a thousand facts of mine cannot抵消(offset) half a sentence of someone else's rumor. It seems that everything that should not be done should be done by women. Even if you haven't done it, they insist that you have done it and don't allow you to defend yourself. So, what methods can we use to provide a reasonable security?

Speaking of which, I have been living under the mercury lamp for quite a few years. At the beginning of this profession, it was nothing more than for the sake of interest and the vertical aspects of life. I never dreamed of the gains I have now at that time, but I also never dreamed of the pain I have now at that time. Therefore, for my contradictory self, I dare not expect anything other than being loyal to my work and seeking protection and trust from my work.

The station. Director Zhang immediately crossed the river to Nanjing to raise overcoats. Fortunately, the Central Military Academy had many coats of discharged officers and soldiers in stock and granted us the right to use them. The problem of keeping warm was slightly resolved. On the 30th, the whole army began to advance.

When the train arrived in Jinan, we were not allowed to get off according to orders. At lunchtime, each person was only given a few pancakes as a meal. One comrade from the South was not used to eating this food. Helplessly, his five internal organs did not cooperate, and he had to force it down. It took him more than thirty minutes. Seeing him so pitiful, I couldn't help but ask him, "Comrade, is it hard for you to eat this?" He said, "No, it's not hard. If the country is destroyed, it will be hard to even want to eat this." How painful these words are!

We will never forget to thank the postal workers everywhere for their love. All the letters of this regiment were delivered properly and quickly. Even documents with only the two words "please deliver" written on the envelope could be查給(checked and given). This made them particularly troublesome. We are really grateful and ashamed.

From Beijing to Ping, the spirit of the entire team remained very strong. Several people joined us along the way. Especially commendable was a comrade who even caught up with us from Suzhou to enlist here in Beiping. Such a sincerity like a huge wave deserves people's praise. But the personality of one comrade was discovered by us to be evil. After discussions by the cadres, it was decided to expel him. A few comrades who could not bear the hardship temporarily asked to return to work in the rear. We did not force them and let them go on their own.

When our regimental headquarters was first established in Shanghai, it was originally intended to serve under General Benma in Heilongjiang. However, now the situation outside the Guan is precarious, and half of the country is about to be destroyed. After discussions by the whole group, everyone agreed that aiding the emergency should be the priority. Therefore, we changed the date to a rally within a few days to cross the Guan and cooperate with the volunteers in Jinxi.

Foreign Rice Sales are Sluggish and Turning Soft 123

Yesterday's foreign rice market situation was that due to the unstable current situation, entries were suspended, and all rice was in a flat and soft situation. Standard Weaving Mills Throwing Becomes Tired 124

Yesterday's market, the morning opening, due to the small quotation of foreign wheat at 2 corners, was unstable for a while. However, because the minds of outsiders are still firm, it has also returned to a clever market. This month, it has reached 1.9 cents. Distant months have also been determined. However, due to the continuous ordering of foreign wheat by factories, they opened in the morning and afternoon and successively released their files. In the afternoon, the sale was even more active, so from February onwards, it gradually fell step by step. According to this situation, if the source of foreign wheat is endless, it seems difficult to ask for a good price, it is said. As a result, this month was 2.5 mils less than the previous day, February was 7.5 mils less, March was 2 cents less, April was 1 cent and 2.5 mils less, May was 7.5 mils less, and June was 1.5 cents less, it is said.

Futures Wheat is the Only Good This Month 125

Yesterday's wheat market generally showed ups and downs in each month after the opening in the morning and afternoon. In early February, it was still flat and tired. Then, due to the scarcity of the delivery volume in this month, foreign empty households were very eager to make up for it, so it was clever and profitable. In the distant future, the price of foreign wheat was still around 2 corners less. It was also reported that a certain factory had continued to order Australian wheat at a price of 3 taels, 7 cents and 1 point. Therefore, people's hearts were not stable, and the deal was finalized yesterday, and the hedging households released their files, causing the trend to soften again. The delivery quantity this month is estimated to be six cars of local wheat collected by Dingtai. It is said that there were more than ten cars of those who giao割 outside the house. As a result, this month was 3 cents better than the previous day, March was 3 cents down, April was immobile, May was 1 cent less, and June was 2 cents less, it is said.
